###########################
# ВЕТКА ТУРКА
###########################

add_namespace = NWturkey

#Претензии на Хатай // FRA
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.1
	title = NWturkey.1.t
	desc = NWturkey.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.1" }
	
	#Оставить Хатай частью Сирии 
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = 3 name = TUR_claims_hatay_threat1_tt }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = diplomatic_affront }
		FROM = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = diplomatic_affront } }
	}
	#Предоставить автономию Хатаю
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		#release = HAT
		if = {
			limit = { event_target:NW_france_scope = { has_full_control_of_state = 945 } }
			HAT = {
				transfer_state = 945
				event_target:NW_france_scope = {
					puppet = HAT
					set_autonomy = { target = HAT autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ideas = HAT_near_autonomy_status
					set_cosmetic_tag = HAT_SANDJAK
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SYR = { has_full_control_of_state = 945 } }
			HAT = {
				transfer_state = 945
				SYR = {
					puppet = HAT
					set_autonomy = { target = HAT autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ideas = HAT_near_autonomy_status
					set_cosmetic_tag = HAT_SANDJAK
				}
			}
		}
		add_named_threat = { threat = -3 name = TUR_claims_hatay_threat2_tt }
		FROM = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = 0.02
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SYR = { exists = yes } }
			SYR = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.73 } }
		}
	}
}


#Монтрё. Приглашение
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.2
	title = NWturkey.2.t
	desc = NWturkey.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.2" }
	
	#Согласиться на переговоры
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ITA
				has_government = fascism
				has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = NWturkey.3 days = 1 }
		set_country_flag = montreux_member_flag
	}
	#Отказаться 
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ITA
				has_government = fascism
				FROM = { has_idea = TUR_fascist_grand_council }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = TUR_the_montreux_convention_cancel
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = TUR_the_montreux_convention_cancel
			}
		}
	}
}

#Монтрё. Голосование
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.3
	title = NWturkey.3.t
	desc = NWturkey.3.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.3" }
	
	#Оставить зону демилитаризированной 
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ITA
				TUR = { has_idea = TUR_fascist_grand_council }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = TUR
			modifier = TUR_the_montreux_convention_abort_demilitariz
		}
		TUR = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = TUR_the_montreux_convention_abort_demilitariz
			}
		}
	}
	#Ремилитаризация зоны 
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { tag = ITA }
				TUR = { has_idea = TUR_fascist_grand_council }
			}
		}
		TUR = { add_to_variable = { montreux_score = 1 } }
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = TUR
			modifier = TUR_the_montreux_convention_accept_demilitariz
		}
		TUR = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = TUR_the_montreux_convention_accept_demilitariz
			}
		}
	}
}

#Монтрё. Итог у турка
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.4
	title = NWturkey.4.t
	desc = NWturkey.4.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.4" }
	
	#Таки ремилитаризация
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.4.a
		trigger = {
			TUR = { check_variable = { var = montreux_score value = 5 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
		}
		341 = { set_demilitarized_zone = no }
		964 = { set_demilitarized_zone = no }
	}
	#Таки слив
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.4.b
		trigger = {
			TUR = { check_variable = { montreux_score < 5 } }
		}
		set_country_flag = dem_montreux_denied
	}
}

#Аннексия Хатая
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.5
	title = NWturkey.5.t
	desc = NWturkey.5.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.5" }
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		TUR = { transfer_state = 945 }
	}
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.5.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					event_target:NW_france_scope = { has_government = democratic }
					GER = { has_government = fascism }
					threat > 0.39
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					event_target:NW_france_scope = { has_government = democratic }
					GER = { has_government = fascism }
					event_target:NW_france_scope = { has_war_with = GER }
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				TUR = { is_in_faction_with = event_target:NW_france_scope }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				event_target:NW_france_scope = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				ENG = { has_guaranteed = TUR }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				FROM = { has_government = ROOT }
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		TUR = { transfer_state = 945 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				TUR = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
				event_target:NW_france_scope = { 
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
					is_faction_leader = no
				}
			}
			event_target:NW_france_scope = { leave_faction = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 945 } }
			945 = {
				owner = {
					TUR = {
						declare_war_on = {
							type = take_state_focus
							target = PREV
							generator = { 945 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { TUR = { NOT = { has_country_flag = tur_hatay_peace_flag } } }
				TUR = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.74 months = 1 } }
			}
		}
	}
}


#Поиск союзников
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.6
	title = NWturkey.6.t
	desc = NWturkey.6.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.6" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.6.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = GER
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				tag = ENG
				OR = {
					GER = {
						exists = yes
						OR = {
							has_government = monarchy
							has_government = fascism
						}
					}
					SOV = {
						exists = yes
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ENG
				FROM = { has_government = fascism }
				has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				tag = GER
				OR = {
					ENG = {
						exists = yes
						has_government = democratic
					}
					SOV = {
						exists = yes
						has_government = communism
					}
				}
				has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = GER
				FROM = { has_government = democratic }
				has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = SOV
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				has_global_flag = NW_TUR_NEW_FOCUS_TREE
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = finding_allies_accept
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.7 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.6.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = ENG
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				has_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = GER
				FROM = { tag = TRK }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.8 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#Восстание курдов в Дерсиме. Спустя год после запрета курдского языка
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.9
	title = NWturkey.9.t
	desc = NWturkey.9.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.9" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.9.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = var:current_party_ideology_group
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_manpower = -5000
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.9.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = var:current_party_ideology_group
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.03
		}
	}
}

#Смерть Ататюрка // 10 ноября 1938 года
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.10
	title = NWturkey.10.t
	desc = NWturkey.10.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_funeral_Ataturk
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.10" }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = ataturk_dead
			if = {
				limit = { neutrality > 0.2 }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = TUR_president_ismet_inenu
						has_completed_focus = TUR_organize_fair_elections
						has_completed_focus = TUR_etchem_circassian_coup
						has_completed_focus = TUR_force_of_order
					}
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_NEUTRAL
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_NEUTRAL_ALTERNATE
						is_historical_focus_on = yes
					}
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 0.42
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = TUR_president_ismet_inenu
						has_completed_focus = TUR_organize_fair_elections
						has_completed_focus = TUR_etchem_circassian_coup
						has_completed_focus = TUR_force_of_order
					}
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_DEMOCRATIC
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_FASCIST
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_TROZKIST
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_COMMUNIST
						has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_MONARCHY
					}
					is_historical_focus_on = no
					neutrality > 0.399
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -1
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 0.15
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.10.a
		capital_scope = { add_manpower = -1 }
		if = {
			limit = { neutrality > 0.2 }
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = -0.1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { name = "Mustafa Kemal Atatürk" }
			}
			kill_country_leader = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_unit_leader = 59 }
			remove_unit_leader = 59
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Mustafa Abdülhalik Renda"
			desc = "POLITICS_MUSTAFA_ABDÜLHALIK_RENDA_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Baskani_Abdulhalik_Renda.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = kemalism
			traits = {
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_president_ismet_inenu
					has_completed_focus = TUR_organize_fair_elections
					has_completed_focus = TUR_etchem_circassian_coup
					has_completed_focus = TUR_force_of_order
				}
				NOT = {
					has_global_flag = WORLD_OF_SPLIT_FLAG
					has_global_flag = THE_MOTHER_OF_ORDER_FLAG
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { neutrality < 0.4 }
				country_event = { id = NWturkey.29 days = 2 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = NWturkey.30 days = 2 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = trworldnews.55 hours = 6 } }
	}
}


#Пантюркизм
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.11
	title = NWturkey.11.t
	desc = NWturkey.11.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.11" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.11.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = guarantee
			active = no
		}
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
				FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		add_threat = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.11.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
	}
}

#Месть Турана // PER
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.12
	title = NWturkey.12.t
	desc = NWturkey.12.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.12" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.12.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		419 = { add_core_of = FROM }
		963 = { add_core_of = FROM }
		FROM = {
			transfer_state = 419
			transfer_state = 963
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = military_access
			active = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			FROM = {
				add_autonomy_score = {
					value = -250
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.12.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.13 days = 1 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = NWturkey_12_b_tt
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.12.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
			419 = { add_claim_by = FROM }
			963 = { add_claim_by = FROM }
			if = {
				limit = { has_guaranteed = FROM }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FROM
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_guaranteed_by = FROM }
				FROM = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = ROOT
						relation = guarantee
						active = no
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				create_wargoal = {
					type = take_state_focus
					target = ROOT
					generator = { 419 963 }
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = conquer
					id = ROOT
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = antagonize
					id = ROOT
					value = 200
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
					FROM = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			FROM = {
				add_autonomy_score = {
					value = 250
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Обмен Турана // TUR
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.13
	title = NWturkey.13.t
	desc = NWturkey.13.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.13" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.13.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		419 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
		963 = { add_core_of = ROOT }
		ROOT = {
			transfer_state = 419
			transfer_state = 963
		}
		FROM = {
			add_political_power = 100
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {

			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				ENG = { has_war = yes }
				ENG = {
					OR = {
						surrender_progress > 0.65
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
				}
				GRE = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
			}
		}
		release_puppet = CYP
	}
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.16.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				ENG = { has_war = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				ENG = { surrender_progress < 0.01 }
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.03
		release = NCP
		NCP = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ENG
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		TUR = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.17 days = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.16.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				ENG = { has_war = yes }
				ENG = {
					OR = {
						surrender_progress > 0.65
						has_capitulated = yes
					}
				}
				GRE = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ENG } }
			}
		}
		GRE = { country_event = { id = NWturkey.19 days = 1 } }
		183 = { add_core_of = GRE }

				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

				has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_NEUTRAL_ALTERNATE
			}
		}
		trigger = { has_civil_war = no }
		
		remove_unit_leader = 1800
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_civwar_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			#add_ideas = TUR_civil_war
			set_country_flag = same_ideology_civil_war_flag
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = fascism
				size = 0.4
				states = { 341 843 964 342 343 339 }

					owner = {
						OR = {
							original_tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							341 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							843 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							964 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
						}
						OR = {
							state = 341
							state = 843
							state = 964
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							342 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							343 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							339 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							340 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
						}
						OR = {
							state = 342
							state = 343
							state = 339
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								341 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								843 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								964 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								342 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								343 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								339 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							}
						}
						OR = {
							state = 341
							state = 843
							state = 964
							state = 342
							state = 343
							state = 339
						}
					}
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = TUR
					has_government = fascism
				}
				#add_ideas = TUR_civil_war
				set_country_flag = same_ideology_civil_war_flag
				set_popularities = {
					neutrality = 95
					fascism = 5
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = TUR_dictatorship_tag
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Fevzi Çakmak"
					desc = "POLITICS_FEVZI_CAKMAK_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/TUR/Portrait_Fevzi_Cakmak.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = kemalism
					traits = { maresal }
				}
				load_focus_tree = { tree = nw_turkish_focus keep_completed = no }
				add_timed_idea = { idea = focus_synchronization days = 7 }
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_president_ismet_inenu
				complete_national_focus = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak
			}
			news_event = { id = trworldnews.56 hours = 6 }
			set_global_flag = cakmak_turkey_civil_war
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.31.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = { has_civil_war = yes }
		
		remove_unit_leader = 1800
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_civwar_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = TUR
				}
				add_core_of = TRK
			}
			
			TRK = {
				#neut
				if = {
					limit = {
						341 = { is_owned_by = TUR }
						843 = { is_owned_by = TUR }
						964 = { is_owned_by = TUR }
					}
					transfer_state = 341
					transfer_state = 843
					transfer_state = 964
				}
				else = {
					transfer_state = 342
					transfer_state = 343
					transfer_state = 339
				}
				
				set_popularities = {
					neutrality = 95
					fascism = 5
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_ideas = generic_civil_war
				set_cosmetic_tag = TUR_dictatorship_tag
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Fevzi Çakmak"
					desc = "POLITICS_FEVZI_CAKMAK_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/TUR/Portrait_Fevzi_Cakmak.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = kemalism
					traits = { maresal }
				}
		
				inherit_technology = TUR
				spawn_tur_civil_war_cakmak = yes
				load_focus_tree = { tree = nw_turkish_focus keep_completed = no }
				add_timed_idea = { idea = focus_synchronization days = 7 }
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_president_ismet_inenu
				complete_national_focus = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ROOT
					type = civil_war
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
				
				#
				if = {
					limit = { TUR = { has_completed_focus = TUR_revolution } }
					add_ideas = TUR_revolution
				}
				if = {
					limit = { TUR = { has_completed_focus = TUR_government_regulation } }
					add_ideas = TUR_government_regulation
				}
				if = {
					limit = { TUR = { has_completed_focus = TUR_varlik_vergisi } }
					add_ideas = TUR_varlik_vergisi
				}
				if = {
					limit = { TUR = { has_completed_focus = TUR_mobilization_eastern_regions } }
					add_ideas = TUR_mobilization_eastern_regions
				}
			}
			news_event = { id = trworldnews.56 hours = 6 }
			set_global_flag = cakmak_trk_turkey_civil_war
		}
	}
}

#Устроить честные выборы
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.33
	title = NWturkey.33.t
	desc = NWturkey.33.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.33" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.33.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = fascism }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				any_country = {
					has_country_flag = hbbrg_flag
					has_government = democratic
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_FASCIST
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = trworldnews.58 hours = 6 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				any_other_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					OR = {
						has_government = democratic
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					NOT = {
						has_government = democratic
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = befriend
						id = ROOT
						value = -100
					}
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = ROOT
						value = -200
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							PER = {
								has_completed_focus = PER_cut_ties_with_europe
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = befriend
							id = "PER"		
							value = 100
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = alliance
							id = "PER"
							value = 200
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_dem_sadabad_flag } }
				set_country_flag = TUR_dem_sadabad_flag
				set_faction_name = TUR_dem_sadabad
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				any_other_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					NOT = {
						has_government = democratic
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.33.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = democratic }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				GER = { has_government = fascism }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				any_country = {
					has_country_flag = hbbrg_flag
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = NW_TUR_AI_DEMOCRATIC
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascism
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = trworldnews.59 hours = 6 } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				any_other_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					OR = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = monarchy
					}
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					NOT = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = monarchy
					}
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = befriend
						id = ROOT
						value = -100
					}
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = ROOT
						value = -200
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							PER = {
								has_completed_focus = PER_cut_ties_with_europe
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = befriend
							id = "PER"		
							value = 100
						}
						add_ai_strategy = {
							type = alliance
							id = "PER"
							value = 200
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_dem_sadabad_flag } }
				set_faction_name = TUR_fas_sadabad
			}
			else = { set_faction_name = TUR_fas_sadabad_2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				any_other_country = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					NOT = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_government = monarchy
					}
				}
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
	}
}

						}
					}

						}
					}

					division_template = {
						name = "Mobile Süvari Tümeni"

						regiments = {
							cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
							cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }

				#}

							OR = {
								original_tag = ROOT
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								341 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								843 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								964 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								340 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							}
							OR = {
								state = 341
								state = 843
								state = 964
								state = 340
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								342 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								343 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								339 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								340 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
							}
							OR = {
								state = 342
								state = 343
								state = 339
								state = 340
							}
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									341 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									843 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									964 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									340 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									342 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									343 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
									339 = { controller = { OR = { original_tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
								}
							}
							OR = {
								state = 341
								state = 843
								state = 964
								state = 340
								state = 342
								state = 343
								state = 339
							}
						}
					}
				}
				
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = TUR
						has_government = neutrality
					}
					load_focus_tree = { tree = nw_turkish_focus keep_completed = no }
					add_timed_idea = { idea = focus_synchronization days = 7 }
					unlock_national_focus = TUR_president_ismet_inenu
					complete_national_focus = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak
					#add_ideas = TUR_civil_war
					set_cosmetic_tag = TUR_dictatorship_tag
					declare_war_on = {
						target = TRK
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = TRK
					create_country_leader = {
						name = "Fevzi Çakmak"
						desc = "POLITICS_FEVZI_CAKMAK_DESC"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/TUR/Portrait_Fevzi_Cakmak.dds"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = kemalism
						traits = { maresal }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_idea = TUR_great_depression }
						remove_ideas = TUR_great_depression
					}
					unlock_national_focus = TUR_president_ismet_inenu
					complete_national_focus = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak
				}
				
				350 = {
					controller = {
						random_other_country = {
							limit = {
								original_tag = TUR
								has_government = neutrality
							}
							declare_war_on = {
								type = civil_war
								target = PREV
							}
							add_civil_war_target = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = TRK }
				TRK = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = TUR
						type = civil_war
					}
					add_civil_war_target = TUR
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = NWturkey.72 days = 150 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.36
	title = NWturkey.36.t
	desc = NWturkey.36.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.36" }

	option = {
		name = NWturkey.36.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				arms_factory > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				arms_factory > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
			}
		}
		
		FROM = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = arms_factory
						size > 2
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
	}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

			has_equipment = { artillery_equipment > 1000 }
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		send_equipment = {

			amount = 3000
			target = FROM
		}

			equipment = artillery_equipment
			amount = 1000
			target = FROM
		}

					}

				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
		send_equipment = {

			amount = 3000
			target = FROM
		}
		send_equipment = {

			amount = 1000
			target = FROM
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.36.d
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = FROM

					original_tag = TUR

			}

			}

country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.42
	title = NWturkey.42.t
	desc = NWturkey.42.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.42" }
	
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		date > 1944.01.01
	}

	option = {
		capital_scope = { add_manpower = -1 }
		name = NWturkey.42.a
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 1801 }
			retire = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = monarchy }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_Abdulmejid_II }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_Abdulmejid_II
					add_idea = TUR_Omer_Faruk_Osmanoglu
				}
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Omer Faruk Osmanoglu"
				desc = "POLITICS_OMER_FARUK_OSMANOGLU_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/TUR/Portrait_Omer_Faruk_Osmanoglu.dds"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = absolute_monarchy
				traits = {
					keep_of_order
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = NWturkey.43.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = TUR }
				TUR = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = TUR
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = TUR modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "TUR"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = PER }
				PER = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = PER
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = PER modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "PER"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = IRQ }
				IRQ = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = IRQ
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = IRQ modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "IRQ"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = AFG }
				AFG = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = AFG
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = AFG modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "AFG"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = EGY }
				EGY = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = EGY
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = EGY modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "EGY"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = SYR }
				SYR = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = SYR
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = SYR modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "SYR"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = BPL }
				BPL = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = BPL
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = BPL modifier = expand_the_sadabat_pact }
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = antagonize
				id = "BPL"
				value = -75
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = PER
				IRQ = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = PER
					is_claimed_by = IRQ
				}
				IRQ = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = IRQ
					is_claimed_by = PER
				}
				PER = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = IRQ
				PER = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = PER
						is_claimed_by = IRQ
					}
					IRQ = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = IRQ
						is_claimed_by = PER
					}
					PER = { remove_state_claim = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		#Новый лидер пакта
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					TUR = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag } }
					PER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag } }
					AFG = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag } }
					IRQ = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag } }
					BPL = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag } }
					EGY = { NOT = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag } }
					NOT = { any_other_country = { has_country_flag = new_saadabad_creator_flag } }
					any_other_country = { has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag }
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = saadabad_accept_flag
						is_in_faction = no
					}
					set_country_flag = new_saadabad_creator_flag
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

			country_event = { id = NWturkey.51 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	#Воспротивиться пакистанскому суверенитету
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.49.b
		trigger = {
			TUR = { check_variable = { var = pakistan_score value = 0 compare = less_than_or_equals } }
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { OR = { has_country_flag = pakistan_konf_accept tag = ENG } }
			country_event = { id = NWturkey.50 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

			add_state_core = 440
			add_state_core = 441

		}

				arms_factory > 0
			}

				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {

			}

				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = -5000
		}

	}

			factor = 25
		}

#Автоивент на начало войнушки
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.57
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.57" }
	
	trigger = {
		threat > 0.499
		tag = RAJ
		RAJ = { has_war = yes }
		TUR = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_full_supply_pak
				has_country_flag = TUR_partial_supply_pak
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.57.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TUR = { has_country_flag = TUR_full_supply_pak } }
			PAK = {
				transfer_state = 443
				transfer_state = 444
				transfer_state = 445
				add_state_core = 443
				add_state_core = 444
				add_state_core = 445
			}
			PAK = { load_oob = "PAK_rebels" }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TUR = { has_country_flag = TUR_partial_supply_pak } }
			PAK = {
				transfer_state = 443
				add_state_core = 443
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TUR = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
			PAK = {
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = befriend
					id = "TUR"			
					value = 200
				}
				add_ai_strategy = {
					type = alliance
					id = "TUR"			
					value = 200
				}
			}
			TUR = { add_to_faction = PAK }
		}
		if = { 
			limit = { TUR = { is_faction_leader = no } }
			PAK = { set_country_flag = pakistan_eng_peace_flag }
			if = {
				limit = { RAJ = { is_subject_of = ENG } }
				ENG = { set_country_flag = eng_pakistan_peace_flag_2 }
			}
			else = {
				RAJ = { set_country_flag = eng_pakistan_peace_flag_2 }
			}
		}
		RAJ = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PAK
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RAJ = { has_civil_war = yes } }
			random_country = {
				limit = { 
					original_tag = RAJ
					NOT = { tag = RAJ }
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PAK
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
}

country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.58
	title = NWturkey.58.t
	desc = NWturkey.58.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.58" }
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.58.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50

		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = { 
				has_war_with = PAK
				is_in_faction_with = ENG
			}
			white_peace = PREV
		}
		PAK = {
			transfer_state = 430
			transfer_state = 440
			transfer_state = 441
			transfer_state = 442
			transfer_state = 443
			transfer_state = 444
			transfer_state = 445
			add_state_core = 430
			add_state_core = 440
			add_state_core = 441
			add_state_core = 442
			add_state_core = 443
			add_state_core = 444
			add_state_core = 445
		}
		RAJ = {
			remove_state_core = 430
			remove_state_core = 440
			remove_state_core = 441
			remove_state_core = 442
			remove_state_core = 443
			remove_state_core = 444
			remove_state_core = 445
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					JAP = { is_faction_leader = yes }
					PAK = { is_in_faction_with = TUR }
					TIB = { is_in_faction_with = TUR }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = TIB
					}
					add_claim_by = JAP
				} 
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.58.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				any_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_war_with = ENG
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				threat > 0.5
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

#Пульсар. Проверка лидера
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.68
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.68" }
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.68.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = GER.influence
					value = 26
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			clear_variable = ENG.influence
			clear_variable = GER.influence
			clear_variable = ENG.discontent
			clear_variable = GER.discontent
			complete_national_focus = TUR_alliance_with_germany
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = ENG.influence
					value = 26
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			clear_variable = ENG.influence
			clear_variable = GER.influence
			clear_variable = ENG.discontent
			clear_variable = GER.discontent

#Сброс нац.духа на ГВ у всех
country_event = {
	id = NWturkey.76
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = turkey_civil_war
			has_global_flag = cakmak_turkey_civil_war
			has_global_flag = cakmak_trk_turkey_civil_war
			has_global_flag = troz_turkey_civil_war
			has_global_flag = mona_turkey_civil_war
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = tcw_over }
		OR = {
			AND = { #Победил Исмет 3х
				TUR = { has_civil_war = no }
				any_other_country = {
					original_tag = TUR
					NOT = { has_government = fascism }
				}
				all_country = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { original_tag = TUR }
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
					}
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = TRK }
			}
			AND = { #Победил Исмет 2х
				TUR = { has_civil_war = no }
				any_other_country = {
					original_tag = TUR
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak }
				}
				all_country = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { original_tag = TUR }
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak }
					}
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = TRK }
			}
			AND = { #Победил Фаш 3х
				TUR = { has_civil_war = no }
				any_other_country = {
					original_tag = TUR
					has_government = fascism
				}
				all_country = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { original_tag = TUR }
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = TRK }
			}
			AND = { #Победил Чакмак 2х
				TUR = { has_civil_war = no }
				any_other_country = {
					original_tag = TUR
					has_completed_focus = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak
				}
				all_country = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { original_tag = TUR }
						has_completed_focus = TUR_dictatorship_cakmak
					}
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = TRK }
			}
			AND = { #Победил Чакмак-TRK
				all_country = {
					NOT = { original_tag = TUR }
				}
				country_exists = TRK
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NWturkey.76" }
	immediate = { set_global_flag = tcw_over }
	
	option = {
		name = NWturkey.76.a
		#every_country = {
		#	limit = { has_idea = TUR_civil_war }
		#	remove_ideas = TUR_civil_war
		#}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.1
	title = NW_new_turkey.1.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.1" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 1
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 1
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_take_credit }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.2 days = 1 } }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NW_new_turkey_1a_tt
	}
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				any_enemy_country = {
					any_controlled_state = { is_core_of = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.3 days = 1 } } }
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = { 
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 2
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 3
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
			add_timed_idea = { idea = TUR_debt_to_eng days = 300 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = SOV } }
			add_timed_idea = { idea = TUR_debt_to_sov days = 300 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
			add_timed_idea = { idea = TUR_debt_to_ger days = 300 }
		}
	}
}

#Турецкий ультиматум // ITA
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.14
	title = NW_new_turkey.14.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.14.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.14" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.14.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = FROM
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = PREV
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { YUG = { is_in_faction_with = FROM } }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					OR = {
						state = 163
						state = 736
						state = 823
						state = 824
					}
				}
				add_core_of = YUG
				YUG = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 164 = { is_owned_by = ROOT } }
			164 = {
				add_core_of = FROM
				FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ALB = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = ALB
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.14.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1 }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = nw_greece.68 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#Ультиматум балканских стран \\ BUL
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.15
	title = NW_new_turkey.15.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.15.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.15" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.15.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_turkish_bulgarian_agreement
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				ROOT = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = PREV
						value = -600
					}
				}
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				ROOT = {
					add_ai_strategy = {
						type = alliance
						id = PREV
						value = -600
					}
				}
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						tag = FROM
						is_in_faction_with = FROM
					}
				}
				OR = {
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
			remove_core_of = ROOT
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = FROM
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = PREV
					NOT = { is_owned_by = PREV }
				}
				PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_core_of = PREV
					NOT = { is_owned_by = PREV }
				}
				PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		48 = { owner = { give_resource_rights = { receiver = FROM state = 48 } } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.15.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.16 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#Состав нового правительства \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.40
	title = NW_new_turkey.40.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.40.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.40" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.40.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_loyalty_inenu_var < 0 } } }
		set_country_flag = TUR_political_despotism_flag
		effect_tooltip = { unlock_national_focus = TUR_political_despotism }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Mustafa Kemal Atatürk" ruling_only = yes } }
				amount_taken_ideas = {
					amount < 3
					slots = { political_advisor }
				}
			}
			add_ideas = TUR_celal_bayar_2
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.40.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		trigger = { has_country_flag = NW_new_turkey_38b_flag }
		set_country_flag = TUR_liberalization_of_political_life_flag
		effect_tooltip = { unlock_national_focus = TUR_liberalization_of_political_life }
		custom_effect_tooltip = NW_new_turkey_40b_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = NW_new_turkey_40_ttt
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			add_ideas = TUR_ali_fethi_okyar
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.40.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes

		}

	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.47
	title = NW_new_turkey.47.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.47.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.47" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.47.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = TUR_accepted_offer_of_concessions }
			FROM = {
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_to_support_economy }
				give_resource_rights = { receiver = ROOT state = 843 }
				give_resource_rights = { receiver = ROOT state = 340 }
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				industrial_complex > 0
			}
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_wargoal_against = FROM }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

		name = NW_new_turkey.57.a

		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Mustafa Abdülhalik Renda"

			picture = "Portrait_Baskani_Abdulhalik_Renda.dds"

			traits = {
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.15
		effect_tooltip = { unlock_national_focus = TUR_political_transformation }
		custom_effect_tooltip = NW_new_turkey_57a_tt
	}
}

#Меджлис избрал Исмета Инёню президентом Турции \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.58
	title = NW_new_turkey.58.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.58.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.58" }
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { communism > 0.099 }
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.59 days = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { democratic > 0.199 }
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.60 days = 10 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { fascism > 0.01 }
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.61 days = 15 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NW_new_turkey_34a_flag
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_revive_the_green_army }
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.62 days = 20 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = NW_new_turkey_34a_flag
					has_completed_focus = TUR_revive_the_green_army
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.64 days = 20 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = TUR_liberalization_of_political_life_flag
						has_country_flag = TUR_bet_on_pan_turkist_flag
						has_country_flag = TUR_building_socialism_flag
						has_country_flag = TUR_reject_statism_flag
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.68 days = 25 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						democratic > 0.299
						has_country_flag = TUR_return_to_islamism_flag
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.69 days = 23 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = TUR_return_to_islamism_flag
					any_unit_leader = {
						has_nationality = ROOT
						operative_leader_mission = counter_intelligence
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.70 days = 25 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = TUR_return_to_islamism_flag
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.71 days = 40 }
			}
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.73 days = 50 }
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.77 days = 65 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.58.a
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Ismet Inönü"
			desc = "POLITICS_ISMET_INÖNÜ_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Turkey_Ismet_Inonu.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = kemalism
			traits = {
				milli_sef
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NW_new_turkey_58a_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = trworldnews.57 hours = 6 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.63
	title = NW_new_turkey.63.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.63.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.63.a
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = trozkism
			size = 0.5
			states = { 352 350 1049 354 355 356 347 }
			states_filter = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						TUR = { has_completed_focus = TUR_evicting_circassians_in_eastern_anatolia }
					}
					OR = {
						state = 352
						state = 350
						state = 1049
						state = 354
					}
				}
				else = {
					OR = {
						state = 352
						state = 350
						state = 355
						state = 356
						state = 347
					}
				}
				
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ROOT
					has_government = trozkism
				}
				load_focus_tree = { tree = nw_turkish_focus_new keep_completed = no }
				add_timed_idea = { idea = focus_synchronization days = 7 }
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_correction_constitution
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_call_for_creation_of_opposition_parties
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_spend_change_of_government
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_support_movement_of_personnel
				complete_national_focus = TUR_revive_the_green_army

		}
	}

				}

					limit = {
						TUR = { has_completed_focus = TUR_evicting_circassians_in_eastern_anatolia }
					}
					OR = {
						state = 352
						state = 350
						state = 1049
						state = 354
					}
				}
				else = {
					OR = {
						state = 352
						state = 350
						state = 355
						state = 356
						state = 347
					}
				}
				
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = ROOT
				has_government = trozkism
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				load_focus_tree = { tree = nw_turkish_focus_new keep_completed = no }

#Правительство требует соблюдать конституцию \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.68
	title = NW_new_turkey.68.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.68.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.68" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.68.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_reject_statism_flag }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = anarchism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_liberalization_of_political_life_flag }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_bet_on_pan_turkist_flag }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_building_socialism_flag }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = TUR_communist_party_relegated_background }
		SOV = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_communist_party_relegated_background } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.68.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_reject_statism_flag }
			add_stability = party_popularity@anarchism
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_liberalization_of_political_life_flag }
			add_stability = party_popularity@democratic
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_bet_on_pan_turkist_flag }
			add_stability = party_popularity@fascism
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_building_socialism_flag }
			add_stability = party_popularity@communism
		}
		add_timed_idea = { idea = TUR_government_resignation days = 30 }
	}
}

						has_government = anarchism

			}

			factor = 50
		}

		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.3
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Fevzi Çakmak"
			desc = "POLITICS_FEVZI_CAKMAK_DESC"

			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = nationalism_ideology
			traits = { maresal }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_civil_war = no
					NOT = { country_exists = KRD }

				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.76 days = 5 }
			}
		}
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.75.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}

		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_civwar_tt

			add_ideas = generic_civil_war

					is_core_of = TUR

			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {

				set_popularities = {
					neutrality = 5
					fascism = 95
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_ideas = generic_civil_war
				set_cosmetic_tag = TUR_dictatorship_tag
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Fevzi Çakmak"
					desc = "POLITICS_FEVZI_CAKMAK_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/TUR/Portrait_Fevzi_Cakmak.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = nationalism_ideology
					traits = { maresal }
				}
				inherit_technology = TUR
				spawn_tur_civil_war_cakmak = yes
				load_focus_tree = { tree = nw_turkish_focus_new keep_completed = no }
				add_timed_idea = { idea = focus_synchronization days = 7 }
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_correction_constitution
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_call_for_creation_of_opposition_parties
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_spend_change_of_government
				complete_national_focus = TUR_bet_on_nationalism
				complete_national_focus = TUR_carry_out_militarization_of_society
				complete_national_focus = TUR_political_transformation
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ROOT
					type = civil_war
				}
				add_civil_war_target = ROOT
			}
			news_event = { id = trworldnews.56 hours = 6 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_civil_war = no
					NOT = { country_exists = KRD }
					any_owned_state = { is_core_of = KRD }
				}
				country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.76 days = 5 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		has_government = fascism
		has_country_leader = { name = "Fevzi Çakmak" ruling_only = yes }
		has_civil_war = no
		NOT = { has_war_with = TRK }
		has_completed_focus = TUR_establish_totalitarianism
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 14
	}

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.120.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		set_party_name = { ideology = fascism name = TUR_fascism_party long_name = TUR_fascism_party }
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Fevzi Çakmak"
			desc = "POLITICS_FEVZI_CAKMAK_DESC"

			traits = { maresal }
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Nihal Atsız"
			desc = "POLITICS_OGUZ_REMZI_ARIK_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/TUR/Portrait_Nihal_Atsiz.dds"

				follower_turkish_nationalism

			factor = 50
		}

	}

			factor = 100

country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.121
	title = NW_new_turkey.121.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.121.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.121" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.121.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 1026
						state = 184
						state = 212
					}
				}
				FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.122 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.121.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.123 days = 1 } }
	}
}

#FROM – территории во Фракии возвращены \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.122
	title = NW_new_turkey.122.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.122.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.122" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.122.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = FROM
				OR = {
					state = 1026
					state = 184
					state = 212
				}
			}
			ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
}

#FROM – отказано в возвращении Фракии \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.123
	title = NW_new_turkey.123.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.123.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.123" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.123.a
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = FROM
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = antagonize
			id = FROM
			value = 200
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = conquer
			id = FROM
			value = 200
		}
	}
}

#Призыв к коалиции с Коммунистической партией Турции \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.127
	title = NW_new_turkey.127.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.127.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.127" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.127.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = NW_new_turkey_127a_tt
		if = {
			limit = { has_opinion_modifier = TUR_communist_party_relegated_background }
			remove_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = TUR_communist_party_relegated_background }
			SOV = { remove_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_communist_party_relegated_background } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.128 days = 10 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.127.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

#Представители Компартии Турции добиваются смены премьер-министра \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.128
	title = NW_new_turkey.128.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.128.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.128" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.128.a
		add_political_power = 50
		set_party_name = { ideology = fascism name = TUR_communism_party long_name = TUR_communism_party_long }
		hidden_effect = { retire_ideology_leader = communism }
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Şefik Hüsnü"
			desc = "POLITICS_SEFIK_HUSNU_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/TUR/Portrait_Turkey_Sefik_Husnu.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = marxism
			traits = {
			    reluctant_stalinist
			}
		}
	}
}

#Турция стала новой республикой Советского Союза \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.130
	title = NW_new_turkey.130.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.130.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.130" }
	immediate = { set_country_flag = NW_new_turkey_129_flag }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.130.a
		FROM = { set_autonomy = { target = ROOT autonomy_state = autonomy_colony } }
		set_cosmetic_tag = TUR_soviet_republic
	}
}

#Отчёт Реджепа Пекера \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.132
	title = NW_new_turkey.132.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.132.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.132" }
	immediate = { set_country_flag = NW_new_turkey_129_flag }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.132.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_fascist_grand_council
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = TUR_fascist_grand_council_op }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = TUR_fascist_grand_council_op }
		GER = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_fascist_grand_council_op } }
		ITA = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_fascist_grand_council_op } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.132.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = TUR_recep_peker_was_fired }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = ENG modifier = TUR_recep_peker_was_fired }
		FRA = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_recep_peker_was_fired } }
		ENG = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = TUR_recep_peker_was_fired } }
	}
}

#Пульсар. Открытие первой консерватории \\ TUR 26 мая 1936 года
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.133
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.133" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.133.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_civil_war = no
				NOT = { has_war_with = TRK }
				
			}
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.134 }
		}
	}
}

#Пульсар. Меджлис рассматривает вариант импичмента президента \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.135
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.135" }
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.135.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = NW_new_turkey_34a_flag }
				check_variable = { TUR_loyalty_anarchists_var < 3 }
				check_variable = { TUR_loyalty_islamists_var < 1 }
				check_variable = { TUR_loyalty_pan_turkists_var < 1 }
				check_variable = { TUR_loyalty_okyar_var < 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_loyalty_chakmak_var < 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_loyalty_inenu_var < 0 }
			}
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.136 }
		}
	}
}

#Меджлис рассматривает вариант импичмента президента \\ TUR

#Импичмент президента \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.137
	title = NW_new_turkey.137.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.137.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.137" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.137.a
		remove_ideas = TUR_political_crisis
		unlock_national_focus = TUR_spend_change_of_government
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Mustafa Abdülhalik Renda"
			desc = "POLITICS_MUSTAFA_ABDÜLHALIK_RENDA_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Baskani_Abdulhalik_Renda.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = kemalism
			traits = {
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = NW_new_turkey.138 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#Выборы президента \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.138
	title = NW_new_turkey.138.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.138.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.138" }

	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.138.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Ismet Inönü"
			desc = "POLITICS_ISMET_INÖNÜ_DESC"
			picture = "Portrait_Turkey_Ismet_Inonu.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = kemalism
			traits = {
				milli_sef
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.138.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		set_country_flag = TUR_liberalization_of_political_life_flag
		effect_tooltip = { unlock_national_focus = TUR_liberalization_of_political_life }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = NW_new_turkey.138.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Fevzi Çakmak"
			desc = "POLITICS_FEVZI_CAKMAK_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/TUR/Portrait_Fevzi_Cakmak.dds"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = nationalism_ideology
			traits = { maresal }
		}
		set_country_flag = TUR_bet_on_fevzi_cakmak_flag
		effect_tooltip = {
			unlock_national_focus = TUR_bet_on_nationalism
			unlock_national_focus = TUR_carry_out_militarization_of_society
		}
	}
}


#TEST \\ TUR
country_event = {
	id = NW_new_turkey.999
	title = NW_new_turkey.999.t
	desc = NW_new_turkey.999.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_rally_3
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): event NW_new_turkey.999" }

	option = {
		name = "TUR NEW FOCUS TREE"
		clr_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
		set_variable = { TUR_loyalty_anarchists_var = 3 }
		load_focus_tree = nw_turkish_focus_new
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "TUR OLD FOCUS TREE"
		set_global_flag = NW_TUR_OLD_FOCUS_TREE
		set_variable = { TUR_loyalty_anarchists_var = 0 }
		load_focus_tree = nw_turkish_focus
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}
